# Diagram: research/orchestrator/tasks/models/shipment_parcel_spark.py


> Auto-generated by Obscura crawlers

## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start]) --> ParseArgs[Parse Command Line Arguments]
    ParseArgs --> InitSpark[Initialize SparkContext & SQLContext]
    InitSpark --> ReadBase[Read Parquet from S3 Input Path]
    ReadBase --> FilterMode[Filter ship_mode_id == 8]
    FilterMode --> SaveRaw[Write Raw Data to Parquet]
    SaveRaw --> ReadRaw[Read Raw Data Back]
    ReadRaw --> LoopModels{For Each Model in MODEL_MAP}
    LoopModels --> AddWindowCols[Add Window Function Columns]
    AddWindowCols --> CalcStats[Calculate std, avg, median, mean]
    CalcStats --> CalcStdDev[Calculate stddev_distance]
    CalcStdDev --> FilterOutliers[Filter stddev_distance between -3.0 and 3.0]
    FilterOutliers --> CalcDeltas[Calculate Time Deltas]
    CalcDeltas --> GroupBy[GroupBy Rollup Keys]
    GroupBy --> Agg30[Aggregate 30 Day Stats]
    Agg30 --> Agg60[Aggregate 60 Day Stats]
    Agg60 --> Agg90[Aggregate 90 Day Stats]
    Agg90 --> Agg120[Aggregate 120 Day Stats]
    Agg120 --> Agg180[Aggregate 180 Day Stats]
    Agg180 --> Agg365[Aggregate 365 Day Stats]
    Agg365 --> WriteModel[Write Model Rollup to Parquet Twice]
    WriteModel --> LoopModels
    LoopModels --> End([End])
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> RawData: Read from S3
    RawData --> FilteredData: Filter ship_mode_id
    FilteredData --> PersistedRaw: Save to Parquet
    PersistedRaw --> EnrichedData: Add Window Functions
    EnrichedData --> CleanedData: Remove Outliers
    CleanedData --> AggregatedData: GroupBy & Aggregate
    AggregatedData --> ModelOutput: Write to S3
    ModelOutput --> [*]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[S3 Input Path] --> B[Base DataFrame]
    C[Shipment Statuses] -.-> B
    D[Orgs Path] -.-> B
    B --> E[Filtered Mode 8]
    E --> F[Raw Data Parquet]
    F --> G[Model Processing]
    G --> H[Model 1: latlng_status_city]
    G --> I[Model 2: latlng_status_city_dayofweek]
    H --> J[Output Parquet 1]
    I --> K[Output Parquet 2]
```
